DROP KEYSPACE hotels;

CREATE KEYSPACE hotels WITH  placement_strategy = 'SimpleStrategy'
AND strategy_options = {replication_factor:1};

USE hotels;

CREATE COLUMN FAMILY content1
WITH comparator = UTF8Type
AND key_validation_class=UTF8Type;

ASSUME content1 validator as utf8;

SET content1['mainpage']['byh']='Book Your Hotel';

SET content1['mainpage']['dst']='Destination';

SET content1['mainpage']['cid']='Check In Date';

SET content1['mainpage']['cod']='Check Out Date';

SET content1['mainpage']['nor']='Rooms';

SET content1['mainpage']['nog']='Guests';:

SET content1['mainpage-es']['byh']='Reserve su hotel';

SET content1['mainpage-es']['dst']='Destino';

SET content1['mainpage-es']['cid']='Llegada Fecha';

SET content1['mainpage-es']['cod']='Fecha de Salida';

SET content1['mainpage-es']['nor']='Habitaciones';

SET content1['mainpage-es']['nog']='Huéspedes';

CREATE COLUMN FAMILY hotelsbycity WITH comparator = 'UTF8Type'
AND key_validation_class=UTF8Type AND column_metadata = [{column_name: hcount, validation_class: UTF8Type} ];

SET hotelsbycity['BLR-IN']['hcount']='20';
